Game Room This is a large room - apparently a later addition to the original house, if the faux wood paneling and hideous mint-green shag carpeting are anything to go by. In the near corner stand a quartet of arcade cabinets, while at the other end of the room, near the entrance to the library, is a pool table; a couple of adventurers are playing a game of 9-ball. Empty and half-empty beer bottles are everywhere. A dartboard hangs on the wall opposite the main egress, which lies to the south. There is a single hole in it. You scan the nametags of your doubles. Not everyone is wearing one, but you do read these: ROC'S NEST, DRAGON, JEWELRY SHOP. The table once occupied by the gamers is no longer in use. Library This is a small room whose walls are lined with overflowing bookcases. At the center of the room are two comfortable-looking chairs, each with a round table beside it; on each table is a lamp. The wall across from the entrance is dominated by a bay window, through which warm light streams. The first alter ego you met sits in one of the chairs, reading his newspaper. It's more than a little alarming to see the hundreds upon hundreds of them just inches away, with nothing visible between you, but the barrier seems to be holding. Among the many trolls crowding the beach is one you recognize from the world of the quest - and while the others have been magically silenced, this one is unaffected by the protection spell. Among the many trolls crowding the beach is one you recognize from the world of the quest - and while the others have been magically silenced, this one is unaffected by the protection spell. "So, I see you've finally come to join your chummy friends!" it sneers. --- speaking to Lonk the troll >>SAY 1 : As opposed to my non-chummy friends? Foyer You are standing in a small area of parquet at the bottom of the stairs. The staircase back up to the second floor lies to the west; a hallway leads north, and this one looks mercifully finite. To the east is a dark room lit by flickering, ghostly light, and the door outside is to the south. > E TV Room The lights are off in this room, but you can still see reasonably well, thanks to the glow of the boxy big-screen television. And what you see is a room full of clones of you, all in adventurers' cloaks, sitting on battered couches watching Rocky IV on Betamax. An archway leads north into the kitchen. You scan the nametags of your doubles. Not everyone is wearing one, but you do read these: TAVERN, DRAGON, TROLLS, DWARVES. (Some of these alternate versions of you are chatting with each other and no one seems to mind.) On the TV, Rocky gives Adrian an early anniversary present, or as he terms it, a "prize." > N Kitchen It looks like this kitchen has been updated piecemeal. The sleek black refrigerator with in-door water and ice dispensers is clearly one of the latest models, while the beige and brown buttons on the wood-grain microwave speak of an earlier generation, and the loudly chugging teal dishwasher a generation before that. The oven is of indeterminate age, though the fact that the clock on it is analog rather than digital suggests a relatively early date. A screen door leads north to the backyard, while an archway to the south will return you to the TV room. One of your doubles tidies up the kitchen. > N Backyard This is a small backyard, marked off by a tall wooden fence. A small patio of volcanic rock tiles plays host to a grill, which a couple of your doubles are tending to, while out on the grass stands a small shed and a recycling bin. A gate leads east. > OPEN GATE That's already open. > E Beach This stretch of beach appears to be under the same bubble of protection as the house; as you look to the south, you can see the shoreline curving away toward the southwest, and hundreds of trolls are struggling to walk up and harass you, but an invisible force holds them back. You are therefore blessedly alone with the sea, the rocks, the thin strand of pebbly sand, and the still, humid air. A pier extends eastward from the shoreline. A small rowboat is tied to the end of it, bobbing as the surf rolls gently in and out. > E An invisible force prevents you from walking out to the end of the pier. > X ROWBOAT The handmade wooden rowboat looks like it was made to seat only one, or possibly two if they're very close friends. Archways to the north and west lead to large rooms full of adventurers in brown cloaks; to the south is a foyer and, beyond that, the front door. > S Foyer You are standing in a small area of parquet at the bottom of the stairs. The staircase back up to the second floor lies to the west; a hallway leads north, and this one looks mercifully finite. The oven is of indeterminate age, though the fact that the clock on it is analog rather than digital suggests a relatively early date. It has the basic furnishings, but little more: a queen bed, bedside table with lamp, dresser with mirror, and, in a nice touch, an overhead ceiling fan. On one side of the bed is a wall safe. On the other side is a large window; the frilly blue curtains are open. Along the adjacent wall, next to the dresser, is a half-open door leading to the bathroom; another door is set into the wall across from the window. You rub your eyes, stretch, and get out of bed. > W Hallway You are standing in a nondescript hallway: plain white walls, a threadbare runner carpet. There is no other end to the hallway; it stretches on forever to the north, with doors at regular intervals. > D You follow the curving staircase downward... [ACTION] north [STATE] Bathroom Even more than the bedroom, this cramped bathroom shows this house's age. Not that it isn't well kept up - it looks like it's been recently cleaned - but the clunky styling of the fixtures suggests that it hasn't been renovated for a couple of generations. Beneath the medicine cabinet is a sink. The far wall is also done in small white tile, chipped here and there. Near that wall, but not attached to it, is a bathtub; however, the towel rack is across the room, above the toilet. Next to the toilet is the doorway, which leads back to the bedroom. [ACTION] east [STATE] TV Room The lights are off in this room, but you can still see reasonably well, thanks to the glow of the boxy big-screen television. And what you see is a room full of clones of you, all in adventurers' cloaks, sitting on battered couches watching Rocky IV on Betamax. An archway leads north into the kitchen. You scan the nametags of your doubles. Not everyone is wearing one, but you do read these: WEAPON SHOP, LABYRINTH, MAGIC, KNIGHTS. (Some of these alternate versions of you are chatting with each other and no one seems to mind.) "Your ability to land your attacks, and to fend off the minotaur's attacks - either by dodging, or blocking them with your shield - depends not just on your dexterity but that of your opponent," your double explains.
